This petition is officially supported by VC firms like Index, Sequoia, Point Nine, Blue Yard, 20VC, Festina, Interface, Speed Invest, Atlantic Labs, Plural, tiny.vc, System.One, FEV, Amino Collective, AENU, Visionaries Club, Launchhub, 2150, HV Capital, K Fund, JME, Lightspeed, Seedcamp, First Momentum, Alliance, Common Magic, Pale Blue Dot, 7percent, Czech Founders, Indico Capital, LocalGlobe, World Fund, Planet A, MIG, Creandum, 4P, Prototype, and many many more. 



We also thank Europe's startup associations for their support in promoting this campaign. Official partners include European Startup Network, Allied for Startups, France Digitale, Dutch Startup Association, Danish Entrepreneurs, Deutscher Startup-Verband, Startup Hungary, Austrian Startups, Adigital, Rise Europe, IE.F, Prompting Europe, EsTech, EBAN, Startup Disrupt, and more.



Additionally, we are proud to be supported by communities like European Women in VC, Station F, Slush, ARRtist, European Defense, Product Hunt, Not Optional, eu/acc, eu·vc, SPRIN-D, ICE, invest.austria, UnternehmerTUM, and more.
